*   Seizing Land from [![Burghers.png](/images/thumb/d/dd/Burghers.png/28px-Burghers.png)](/Burghers "Burghers")Burghers no longer triggers [![Particularist rebels.png](/images/thumb/8/85/Particularist_rebels.png/24px-Particularist_rebels.png)](/Particularists "Particularists")Revolts

  

**Mercantilistic Approach**

*   [![Cost to promote mercantilism.png](/images/thumb/c/c1/Cost_to_promote_mercantilism.png/28px-Cost_to_promote_mercantilism.png)](/Cost_to_promote_mercantilism "Cost to promote mercantilism") **−10%** Cost to promote mercantilism
*   [![Trade power.png](/images/thumb/1/10/Trade_power.png/28px-Trade_power.png)](/Domestic_trade_power "Domestic trade power") **+15%** Domestic trade power
*   [![Merchant trade power.png](/images/thumb/3/39/Merchant_trade_power.png/28px-Merchant_trade_power.png)](/Merchant_trade_power "Merchant trade power") **+5** Merchant trade power

![Mercantilistic Approach icon](/images/thumb/9/93/Gov_paper_with_seal.png/40px-Gov_paper_with_seal.png "Mercantilistic Approach icon")

Free trade implies an equal relation between imports and exports of goods. While beneficial for certain goods, it is of little value for our state. Only through maximizing our exports while minimizing the import from foreign powers, our state can grow its economy.

**Conditions:**

*   Is _not_ a [![Gov pirate republic.png](/images/thumb/1/11/Gov_pirate_republic.png/28px-Gov_pirate_republic.png)](/Pirate_republic "Pirate republic") ‘Pirate Republic’

* * *

**Additional effects:**

*   The Privilege "Indepted to the Burghers" no longer lowers [![Mercantilism.png](/images/thumb/0/05/Mercantilism.png/28px-Mercantilism.png)](/Mercantilism "Mercantilism")Mercantilism

  

**Embrace Free Trade**

*   [![Institution spread.png](/images/thumb/b/bb/Institution_spread.png/28px-Institution_spread.png)](/Institution_spread "Institution spread") **+25%** Institution spread
*   [![Trade power abroad.png](/images/thumb/a/a9/Trade_power_abroad.png/28px-Trade_power_abroad.png)](/Trade_power_abroad "Trade power abroad") **+20%** Trade power abroad

![Embrace Free Trade icon](/images/thumb/8/8f/Gov_merchant.png/40px-Gov_merchant.png "Embrace Free Trade icon")

Merchants from all of the world should be able to travel into our lands to engage with our population in trade and commerce. Abandoning the narrowness of mercantalism, the state gains an easier access to foreign thoughts.

**Conditions:**

*   Is _not_ a [![Gov pirate republic.png](/images/thumb/1/11/Gov_pirate_republic.png/28px-Gov_pirate_republic.png)](/Pirate_republic "Pirate republic") ‘Pirate Republic’

* * *

**Additional effects:**

*   Gain [![All power costs.png](/images/thumb/0/0f/All_power_costs.png/28px-All_power_costs.png)](/Monarch_power "Monarch power")**100** of every Monarch Power when [![Institutions.png](/images/thumb/4/43/Institutions.png/28px-Institutions.png)](/Institutions "Institutions") embracing an Institution

[![Cradle of Civilization.png](/images/thumb/2/23/Cradle_of_Civilization.png/28px-Cradle_of_Civilization.png)](/Cradle_of_Civilization "Cradle of Civilization")

Available only with the [Cradle of Civilization](/Cradle_of_Civilization "Cradle of Civilization") DLC enabled.

*   The Trading Policy "Improve Inland Routes" no longer requires [![Trade power.png](/images/thumb/1/10/Trade_power.png/28px-Trade_power.png)](/Trade_power "Trade power")Trade Power

  

**Embrace the Economic Theory**

*   [![Interest per annum.png](/images/thumb/f/fc/Interest_per_annum.png/28px-Interest_per_annum.png)](/Interest_per_annum "Interest per annum") **\-0.5** Interest per Annum

![Embrace the Economic Theory icon](/images/thumb/8/8a/Gov_dutch_flag.png/40px-Gov_dutch_flag.png "Embrace the Economic Theory icon")

The economy plays an undeniably important role within the apparatus of the state. The complex systems of trade, finance and luxury need to be tamed to serve the health of the government.

**Conditions:**

*   Is _not_ a [![Gov pirate republic.png](/images/thumb/1/11/Gov_pirate_republic.png/28px-Gov_pirate_republic.png)](/Pirate_republic "Pirate republic") ‘Pirate Republic’

  

**Lockean Proviso**

*   [![Development cost.png](/images/thumb/a/a2/Development_cost.png/28px-Development_cost.png)](/Development_cost "Development cost") **−5%** Development cost
*   [![Goods produced modifier.png](/images/thumb/1/12/Goods_produced_modifier.png/28px-Goods_produced_modifier.png)](/Goods_produced_modifier "Goods produced modifier") **+5%** Goods produced modifier

![Lockean Proviso icon](/images/thumb/e/e8/Gov_paper_money_map.png/40px-Gov_paper_money_map.png "Lockean Proviso icon")

Unused property is a waste to both nature and the state. By introducing and emphasizing hard goods which yield utility over periods of time, the people can exchange their exessive possessions without offending the natural law. The government would moderate the conflict between accumulation of property and distribution of wealth.

**Conditions:**

*   Is _not_ a [![Gov pirate republic.png](/images/thumb/1/11/Gov_pirate_republic.png/28px-Gov_pirate_republic.png)](/Pirate_republic "Pirate republic") ‘Pirate Republic’
*   Has completed [![Economic idea group.png](/images/thumb/9/9d/Economic_idea_group.png/28px-Economic_idea_group.png)](/Economic_ideas "Economic ideas") Economic Ideas or [![Infrastructure idea group.png](/images/thumb/b/b3/Infrastructure_idea_group.png/28px-Infrastructure_idea_group.png)](/Infrastructure_ideas "Infrastructure ideas") Infrastructure Ideas

The resources of the New World are plenty and of great value. By granting certain rights and privileges to our merchants, we can assure that these foreign goods are exploited and transported to our state, which we then distribute in the Old World.

**Conditions:**

Thalassocracy, Rule by The Sea. Ours is a people whose lives are lived out with, by and for the sea. Our empire stretches far beyond our homeland and into far-flung colonies in our extended Outremer, our Lands Beyond The Sea. From coast to coasts beyond, our flags wave from ships upon the briny foam. The sea is cold, yet we have made it our home. Let no one challenge us in our proper element.

To be a Sikh means to be a student, and by learning from these wise men and studying the works of the great Gurus of the Sikh religion, we may spread our enlightened vision across the world.

### Separation of Powers\[[edit](/index.php?title=Theocracy&veaction=edit&section=15 "Edit section: Separation of Powers") | [edit source](/index.php?title=Theocracy&action=edit&section=15 "Edit section: Separation of Powers")\]

Effects

Description & notes

**Clerical Commission**

We should divide the powers of the state between our religious leader and a commission of clerics. This commission will be charged with keeping the peace in our nation, and conducting diplomatic affairs on our leader’s behalf.

**Divine Guidance**

The people question if we should divide the power in our nation, but the power is already divided. The true leader of our state is divine in nature, and their will is interpreted by our leader here on Earth.

**Constitutional Theocracy**

*   [![Years of separatism.png](/images/thumb/a/a2/Years_of_separatism.png/28px-Years_of_separatism.png)](/Years_of_separatism "Years of separatism") **−10** Years of separatism

**Theocratic Democracy**

*   [![National unrest.png](/images/thumb/8/8d/National_unrest.png/28px-National_unrest.png)](/National_unrest "National unrest") **−1** National unrest

![Theocratic Democracy icon](/images/thumb/4/47/Gov_assembly_hall.png/40px-Gov_assembly_hall.png "Theocratic Democracy icon")

We are divinest of all, but we must never forget the inherent divinity found in even the lowliest of commoners. By allowing our peasants to elect their own representatives, we allow them to have their own voice in the court of the divine.

**Conditions:**

*   Not available with [Monastic Order](/Theocracy#Monastic_Order "Theocracy") reform or as [![Flag of Jerusalem](/images/thumb/e/ef/Jerusalem.png/20px-Jerusalem.png)](/Jerusalem "Jerusalem") [Jerusalem](/Jerusalem "Jerusalem").
*   Only available if the [![Nobility.png](/images/thumb/c/c8/Nobility.png/28px-Nobility.png)](/Nobility "Nobility")Nobility estate does not exist or if the [![Crownland.png](/images/thumb/e/ed/Crownland.png/28px-Crownland.png)](/Crown_land "Crown land") Crown owns more lands than the [![Nobility.png](/images/thumb/c/c8/Nobility.png/28px-Nobility.png)](/Nobility "Nobility")Nobility estate and the [![Nobility loyalty equilibrium.png](/images/thumb/f/f9/Nobility_loyalty_equilibrium.png/28px-Nobility_loyalty_equilibrium.png)](/Nobility_loyalty_equilibrium "Nobility loyalty equilibrium") Nobility loyalty is equal or higher than their [![Nobility influence.png](/images/thumb/9/91/Nobility_influence.png/28px-Nobility_influence.png)](/Nobility_influence "Nobility influence") influence.

* * *

**Additional Effects:**

[![Common Sense.png](/images/thumb/e/e4/Common_Sense.png/28px-Common_Sense.png)](/Common_Sense "Common Sense")

Available only with the [Common Sense](/Common_Sense "Common Sense") DLC enabled.

*   Enables [![Parliament.png](/images/thumb/f/f9/Parliament.png/28px-Parliament.png)](/Parliament "Parliament") parliament
*   Disables the [![Nobility.png](/images/thumb/c/c8/Nobility.png/28px-Nobility.png)](/Nobility "Nobility") nobility estate
*   Disables Call Diet

**Regionally Elected Commanders**

*   [![National unrest.png](/images/thumb/8/8d/National_unrest.png/28px-National_unrest.png)](/National_unrest "National unrest") **−1** National unrest

![Regionally Elected Commanders icon](/images/thumb/0/03/Reform_regionally_elected_commanders.png/40px-Reform_regionally_elected_commanders.png "Regionally Elected Commanders icon")

In our government, the successor to the current ruler is decided by a vote from the warriors who have dedicated their lives to protecting the Faith. By allowing the citizens of the towns and villages under our protection to partake in electing the Commander that represents their interests, we may begin to expand our administration and make those under our protection feel accurately represented in the Court of Commanders.

**Conditions:**

*   Only available for [Monastic Order](/Theocracy#Monastic_Order "Theocracy")s or as [![Flag of Jerusalem](/images/thumb/e/ef/Jerusalem.png/20px-Jerusalem.png)](/Jerusalem "Jerusalem") [Jerusalem](/Jerusalem "Jerusalem").
*   Only available if the [![Nobility.png](/images/thumb/c/c8/Nobility.png/28px-Nobility.png)](/Nobility "Nobility")Nobility estate does not exist or if the [![Crownland.png](/images/thumb/e/ed/Crownland.png/28px-Crownland.png)](/Crown_land "Crown land") Crown owns more lands than the [![Nobility.png](/images/thumb/c/c8/Nobility.png/28px-Nobility.png)](/Nobility "Nobility")Nobility estate and the [![Nobility loyalty equilibrium.png](/images/thumb/f/f9/Nobility_loyalty_equilibrium.png/28px-Nobility_loyalty_equilibrium.png)](/Nobility_loyalty_equilibrium "Nobility loyalty equilibrium") Nobility loyalty is equal or higher than their [![Nobility influence.png](/images/thumb/9/91/Nobility_influence.png/28px-Nobility_influence.png)](/Nobility_influence "Nobility influence") influence.

* * *

**Additional Effects:**

*   Unlocks the ability to change government rank.

[![Common Sense.png](/images/thumb/e/e4/Common_Sense.png/28px-Common_Sense.png)](/Common_Sense "Common Sense")

Available only with the [Common Sense](/Common_Sense "Common Sense") DLC enabled.

*   Enables [![Parliament.png](/images/thumb/f/f9/Parliament.png/28px-Parliament.png)](/Parliament "Parliament") parliament
*   Disables the [![Nobility.png](/images/thumb/c/c8/Nobility.png/28px-Nobility.png)](/Nobility "Nobility") nobility estate
*   Disables Call Diet

**Open Public Elections**

*   [![Stability cost modifier.png](/images/thumb/e/eb/Stability_cost_modifier.png/28px-Stability_cost_modifier.png)](/Stability_cost_modifier "Stability cost modifier") **−15%** Stability cost modifier

![Open Public Elections icon](/images/thumb/0/03/Reform_monastic_elections.png/40px-Reform_monastic_elections.png "Open Public Elections icon")

Many villages under our protection demand representation, and although they are fools who do not understand that the Commander’s rulership is divine, we must grant them some concessions if we are to keep them happy. Traditionally, only Commanders would vote for the new leader of our Order, but by opening elections to the public and establishing two new subdivisions of our Order for the people to vote for, they may feel their interests are represented by the state.

**Additional Effects:**

*   Unlocks the ability to change Government rank.

[![Res Publica.png](/images/thumb/b/b5/Res_Publica.png/28px-Res_Publica.png)](/Res_Publica "Res Publica")

Available only with the [Res Publica](/Res_Publica "Res Publica") DLC enabled.

*   Elections held every 4 years and when the ruler dies
*   Does not have Heirs.
*   Enables Militarists and Theocrats mechanics
*   Choice between a Militarist and a Theocrat candidate with random stats and no re-election possible, each side gathering power from the player's choices. You can see their stats before choosing

**A Dynastic Theocracy**

*   [![Land leader fire.png](/images/thumb/2/27/Land_leader_fire.png/28px-Land_leader_fire.png)](/Land_leader_fire "Land leader fire") **+1** Land leader fire
*   [![Harsh treatment cost.png](/images/thumb/7/7d/Harsh_treatment_cost.png/28px-Harsh_treatment_cost.png)](/Harsh_treatment_cost "Harsh treatment cost") **−20%** Harsh treatment cost
*   [![Yearly devotion.png](/images/thumb/9/9d/Yearly_devotion.png/28px-Yearly_devotion.png)](/Yearly_devotion "Yearly devotion") **+0.25** Yearly devotion

![A Dynastic Theocracy icon](/images/thumb/2/2f/Reform_commander_king.png/40px-Reform_commander_king.png "A Dynastic Theocracy icon")

Faith will always play a vital role in our state, but it is becoming clear that our government is not adaptable enough to rule vast swathes of land and function in this changing world. There is no reason that our men of faith must swear themselves into celibacy and by reorganizing our state into a Dynastic Theocracy and granting our rulers royal titles, we will become protectors of the faith and the crown, guided by our Theocratic King.

**Additional Effects:**

*   Unlocks the ability to change Government rank.
*   Does not have heir.
*   Has consort.
*   Allows Royal marriage.
*   A [![General.png](/images/thumb/6/6d/General.png/28px-General.png)](/General "General") General becomes ruler when the current ruler dies.

**Lords of the Sea**

*   [![Yearly devotion.png](/images/thumb/9/9d/Yearly_devotion.png/28px-Yearly_devotion.png)](/Yearly_devotion "Yearly devotion") **+0.25** Yearly devotion
*   [![Naval leader fire.png](/images/thumb/4/41/Naval_leader_fire.png/28px-Naval_leader_fire.png)](/Naval_leader_fire "Naval leader fire") **+1** Naval leader fire
*   [![Morale of navies.png](/images/thumb/8/80/Morale_of_navies.png/28px-Morale_of_navies.png)](/Morale_of_navies "Morale of navies") **+15%** Naval morale

![Lords of the Sea icon](/images/thumb/f/f2/Reform_admiral_king.png/40px-Reform_admiral_king.png "Lords of the Sea icon")

The good work our soldiers have done in securing safe passage for pilgrims across the sea has made our sails a feared sight for pirates and heathens alike. However, it has become clear that the threat pirates pose to our faith go far beyond our small shores, and we must expand our order to become an Empire in itself if we are to properly serve our holy mission. By enacting a series of reforms within our government, we shall vastly expand our administration beyond our borders and our valiant Knights will elect all future commanders based on the number of pirate lords they have brought to kneel before God!

**Conditions:**

*   capital has a port

* * *

**Additional Effects:**

*   Unlocks the ability to change Government rank.
*   Does not have an heir.
*   Has consort.
*   Allows [royal marriages](/Royal_marriage "Royal marriage").
*   An [![Admiral.png](/images/thumb/d/d1/Admiral.png/28px-Admiral.png)](/Admiral "Admiral") Admiral becomes ruler when the current ruler dies.

### The Nature of Our Faith\[[edit](/index.php?title=Theocracy&veaction=edit&section=16 "Edit section: The Nature of Our Faith") | [edit source](/index.php?title=Theocracy&action=edit&section=16 "Edit section: The Nature of Our Faith")\]

Effects

Description & notes

**Faith and Power**

*   [![Morale damage received.png](/images/thumb/d/d0/Morale_damage_received.png/28px-Morale_damage_received.png)](/Morale_damage_received "Morale damage received") **−10%** Morale damage received

![Faith and Power icon](/images/thumb/1/1f/Gov_soldiers_5.png/40px-Gov_soldiers_5.png "Faith and Power icon")

Combat and power are the only ways to come closer to divine. Through victories on the battlefield, the people of our state show their piety and devotion.

**Additional Effects:**

*   Winning battles which are leada by our Ruler increases Devotion by **0.5** and Absolutism by **0.1**

Faith is the unifying power which keeps the state and the people together. The government exists for the mere purpose to ensure that this unity remains unbroken.

![God and Man icon](/images/thumb/2/2e/Gov_religious_leader.png/40px-Gov_religious_leader.png "God and Man icon")

The only relationship that matters is that between lowly mortals and the immortal holy spirits. Our state exists merely to remind people of the proper ways to devote themselves to prayer.

**Conditions:**

*   is NOT in [Pagan](/Pagan_denominations "Pagan denominations") religion group.

**Organize Our Faith**

*   [![Yearly devotion.png](/images/thumb/9/9d/Yearly_devotion.png/28px-Yearly_devotion.png)](/Yearly_devotion "Yearly devotion") **+1** Yearly devotion

We are a highly organized state oriented around a faith that is itself highly disorganized. By attempting to enact an official hierarchy for our religion, we may begin to convert more followers to the true ways of the Gods.

**Conditions:**

*   is in [Pagan](/Pagan_denominations "Pagan denominations") religion group.

**Soul and Body**

*   [![Tolerance heretic.png](/images/thumb/2/27/Tolerance_heretic.png/28px-Tolerance_heretic.png)](/Tolerance_of_heretics "Tolerance of heretics") **+1** Tolerance of Heretics

![Soul and Body icon](/images/thumb/0/02/Reform_religious_harmony.png/40px-Reform_religious_harmony.png "Soul and Body icon")

We must never forget that the barriers of culture and language are merely an illusion. We are all mere souls inhabiting a shell. It does not matter what language we speak, only that we service the divine in the proper way.

**Conditions:**

*   is [![Confucianism](/images/thumb/a/a2/Confucianism.png/28px-Confucianism.png)](/Confucian "Confucian") Confician

### Culture, Faith and State\[[edit](/index.php?title=Theocracy&veaction=edit&section=17 "Edit section: Culture, Faith and State") | [edit source](/index.php?title=Theocracy&action=edit&section=17 "Edit section: Culture, Faith and State")\]

Type

Effects

Description & notes

**Religious Society**

*   [![Governing capacity modifier](/images/thumb/8/84/Governing_capacity_modifier.png/28px-Governing_capacity_modifier.png)](/Governing_capacity "Governing capacity modifier") **+250** Governing Capacity

![Religious Society icon](/images/thumb/6/6e/Reform_mission_to_civilize.png/40px-Reform_mission_to_civilize.png "Religious Society icon")

Religion and culture are intertwined. No man of our society can claim to be of our culture if they do not follow the same rituals.

**Harmonization of Cultures**

*   [![Promote culture cost.png](/images/thumb/7/76/Promote_culture_cost.png/28px-Promote_culture_cost.png)](/Promote_culture_cost "Promote culture cost") **−50%** Promote culture cost

![Harmonization of Cultures icon](/images/thumb/9/96/Gov_generic_people.png/40px-Gov_generic_people.png "Harmonization of Cultures icon")

The concept of culture is in many ways similar to religion, though it is forged by traditions, social values and environment and not by divine enlightenment. The cultures within our state are bound to harmonize with each other as long they are following the true faith.

**Cultural Safe Haven**

*   [![Manpower.png](/images/thumb/0/0c/Manpower.png/28px-Manpower.png)](/Manpower "Manpower")[![Culture icon.png](/images/thumb/2/29/Culture_icon.png/28px-Culture_icon.png)](/Culture "Culture") **+10%** Manpower in accepted culture provinces
*   [![Manpower.png](/images/thumb/0/0c/Manpower.png/28px-Manpower.png)](/Manpower "Manpower") [![Primary culture.png](/images/thumb/e/e1/Primary_culture.png/28px-Primary_culture.png)](/Primary_culture "Primary culture")**+10%** Manpower in same culture group provinces

![Cultural Safe Haven icon](/images/thumb/b/b6/Gov_man_and_children.png/40px-Gov_man_and_children.png "Cultural Safe Haven icon")

Cultures are fabricated social norms, created by men to differentiate them from others. In actuality, we are all mortal bodies walking on this world. Only the conviction to the true divine being is of importance.

**Taxation of Foreigners**

*   [![National tax modifier.png](/images/thumb/3/34/National_tax_modifier.png/28px-National_tax_modifier.png)](/National_tax_modifier "National tax modifier") **+50%** National tax modifier

![Taxation of Foreigners icon](/images/thumb/8/81/Reform_government_for_people.png/40px-Reform_government_for_people.png "Taxation of Foreigners icon")

The culture of minorities is of little concern to us. As long they are willing to sacrifice part of their income for the holy cause, they are free to live out their traditions.

**Additional Effects:**

[![Cradle of Civilization.png](/images/thumb/2/23/Cradle_of_Civilization.png/28px-Cradle_of_Civilization.png)](/Cradle_of_Civilization "Cradle of Civilization")

Description & notes

**Priestly Autonomy**

*   [![Administrative efficiency.png](/images/thumb/6/6e/Administrative_efficiency.png/28px-Administrative_efficiency.png)](/Administrative_efficiency "Administrative efficiency") **+2.5%** Administrative Efficiency

No priest should hold power over another priest, with the exception of our ruler. Each realm shall be fully autonomous, and priests will remain free to interpret the will of the Gods in any way that is true to them.

**State of Theologians**

Our religion is no weapon or justification of war. Nor does it exist for monetary sake. Our faith is the result of intellectual and spiritual theories, discussions and understanding. The theology is the purpose of the state and its subjects.

Our faith and our state have become totally synonymous with each other. We are our religion, and any who devote themselves to the divine, must also devote themselves to the state.

This world is full of heretics, heathens, sinners, and blasphemers! We must seek to correct heretics and heathens alike, and spread our peaceful ways through force!

We believe that there is only one God, by whom we live and by whom we die, and for whom we have an upright heart. But as God gives us the different fingers of the hand, so he gives to men diverse ways to approach him.

*   Only available if the religion is [![Tengri](/images/thumb/9/9f/Tengri.png/28px-Tengri.png)](/Tengri "Tengri") tengri.

  

**Table of Ranks**

*   [![Administrative efficiency.png](/images/thumb/6/6e/Administrative_efficiency.png/28px-Administrative_efficiency.png)](/Administrative_efficiency "Administrative efficiency") **+2.5%** Administrative efficiency
*   [![Free policies.png](/images/thumb/7/79/Free_policies.png/28px-Free_policies.png)](/Free_policies "Free policies") **+1** Free policies

![Table of Ranks icon](/images/thumb/3/31/Gov_imperial_russia.png/40px-Gov_imperial_russia.png "Table of Ranks icon")

The Empire needs a strong rulership free from the ambitions and intrigues of the boyars. The Table of Ranks restructures the hierarchical system of the Nobility, rewarding merit in the matters of military, bureaucracy and other subjects of the government. The nobles are bound to the Emperor by their personal service.

**Conditions** :

[![Domination.png](/images/thumb/3/3d/Domination.png/28px-Domination.png)](/Domination "Domination")

Available only with the [Domination](/Domination "Domination") DLC enabled.

*   Is _not_ [![Gov pirate republic.png](/images/thumb/1/11/Gov_pirate_republic.png/28px-Gov_pirate_republic.png)](/Pirate_republic "Pirate republic") a Pirate Republic
*   Was unlocked via the [![Flag of Russia](/images/thumb/e/ee/Russia.png/20px-Russia.png)](/Russia "Russia") Russian [![Mission.png](/images/thumb/2/29/Mission.png/24px-Mission.png)](/Missions "Missions") mission "The Table of ranks"

* * *

**Additional effects** :

*   [![Tab domestic government.png](/images/thumb/f/ff/Tab_domestic_government.png/28px-Tab_domestic_government.png)](/Government "Government") Enables ‘Table of Ranks’ interactions:

Icon

Ability

Cost

Effects

[![Table of ranks adm button.png](/images/thumb/b/ba/Table_of_ranks_adm_button.png/48px-Table_of_ranks_adm_button.png)](/File:Table_of_ranks_adm_button.png)

Appoint Chancellor

[![Administrative power.png](/images/e/ef/Administrative_power.png)](/Administrative_power "Administrative power")45

An Advisor of your Choice will join the court. This Advisor will be **50%** cheaper to employ.

[![Table of ranks dip button.png](/images/thumb/1/1d/Table_of_ranks_dip_button.png/48px-Table_of_ranks_dip_button.png)](/File:Table_of_ranks_dip_button.png)

Appoint General Admiral

[![Navy tradition.png](/images/c/cd/Navy_tradition.png)](/Navy_tradition "Navy tradition")10

Gain an [![Admiral.png](/images/thumb/d/d1/Admiral.png/28px-Admiral.png)](/Admiral "Admiral")Admiral with **100** Tradition. This Admiral will additionally gain **+1**[![Naval leader fire.png](/images/thumb/4/41/Naval_leader_fire.png/28px-Naval_leader_fire.png)](/Naval_leader_fire "Naval leader fire") Fire and **+2**[![Naval leader maneuver.png](/images/thumb/4/4a/Naval_leader_maneuver.png/28px-Naval_leader_maneuver.png)](/Naval_leader_maneuver "Naval leader maneuver") Maneuver pips.

[![Table of ranks mil button.png](/images/thumb/1/1e/Table_of_ranks_mil_button.png/48px-Table_of_ranks_mil_button.png)](/File:Table_of_ranks_mil_button.png)

Appoint General Field Marshal

[![Army tradition.png](/images/8/8d/Army_tradition.png)](/Army_tradition "Army tradition")10

Gain an [![General.png](/images/thumb/6/6d/General.png/28px-General.png)](/General "General")General with **100** Tradition. This Admiral will additionally gain **+1**[![Leader siege.png](/images/thumb/6/60/Leader_siege.png/28px-Leader_siege.png)](/Leader_siege "Leader siege") Siege and **+2**[![Land leader fire.png](/images/thumb/2/27/Land_leader_fire.png/28px-Land_leader_fire.png)](/Land_leader_fire "Land leader fire") Fire pips.
